< Text>
You can call in your order, order it online or use Doordash for this location.  Any of these means is easy to use.  Never had food late from here, always made to order.  I don't think they have a heated warmer to keep the pizza hot before pick up, just a padded bag.  Place is clean and staff is polite.  They have a few tables if you want to done in with a few TVs running.  Haven't had a parking issue when I visited, place is easy to spot from the road.<//Text>

< Text>
I order pizza from Via mia  sometimes in Saturday afternoon after my sons soccer team games, they have Halal meat. The pizza is terrific. they have wide range of choice, I would prefer to order the combination pizza that includes mozzarella cheese, salami,pepperoni, mushrooms, lingiica,peppers, black olives, italian sausage and ground beef.
also they have another pizza called All Meat, they add all meat toppings with vegetables.

The service was fast and the team are friendly. the only disadvantage for me is they closed a good location in Santa clara (due to a fire in the plaza) the older location was better than the new one and off course closer to my home.</Text>

< Text>

<Response>None< /Response>< review>
Parking:  Difficult street, paid lots (medium difficulty)

Came here on a Thursday night and at 5PM, the only opening was at 7PM.

I ordered the

-Truffle mushrooms (THIS IS WHAT I WOULD RETURN FOR.. THIS WAS DELICIOUS).  They tasted like dry portobellos, lightly grilled or spritzed with truffle oil.  SO GOOD. Definitely recommend this overpriced dish.
I would order these mushrooms again 100%.

-Meatballs were really tender.  Soft and the sauce was not overpowering at all.  However, nothing special.

-Ordered the lobster ravioli.  Really good but wouldn't order it again.  The sauce was tasty and lightly salted.  The ravioli skin was really delicate and had the perfect amount of chew.

-Langostines. They were good and I think VERY LIGHTLY SEASONED.  To me, this should be more of an appetizer since all the other dishes overpowered this one.  However, the meat was tender and great to try..  Try once but that's all I would recommend.

Final verdict:  I would return ONLY for the truffle mushrooms... MMMMM</review>

<user>102720428694147093759< /user><GmapID>0x80c2bace1d2a445f:0x3f9a1fb54c8e9ca6<//GmapID><pictures>None</pictures>< review>
My first time at the beautiful Via a Veneto last night. It was our 29th wedding anniversary and we were celebrating with four nights at Shutters On The Beach and dinners in a variety of different restaurants in Santa Monica. First, we are a well travelled couple. Second, I am Italian and a foodie. Dining at Via Veneto was like being in Italy. Entire staff is Italian... charming, sweet and very warm. Service was impeccable. The food was spectacularly delicious. My husband had the burata, heirloom tomato and prosciutto to start and veal Milanese for his entree. My appetizer was a duo of fresh salmon tartare and fresh ahi tuna tartare. Both tartare were made with olive oil and was very delicious and so fresh. My entree was a porcini veal scalloping. It was mouthwateringly divine. For dessert we split the panna cotta with fresh berries and Nutella. Everything was wonderful. The restaurant itself is beautifully lit be three chandeliers and the room is intimate. One of the nicest things about Via Veneto is that it‚Äôs not noisy. One can have a conversation without shouting. We just loved it and will be coming back soon. You must make a reservation. This restaurant is a little gem and is always booked. Be warned however, it is not an inexpensive restaurant but I believe that you get what you pay for and Via Veneto definitely delivers.<//review>

< text>
Very friendly atmosphere. There was a sort of limited selection of fresh fruits and vegetables when I went, and one fresh flower stand. The majority of the market is comprised of a variety of prepared foods and drinks (ex: Korean BBQ, artisan grilled cheese, Poke, Indian, Mediterranean...stuff like that). There was also two places to get fresh eggs and one of those places also sold fresh meat. In addition to that there were a few booths with non-food items like candles‚Äã, lotion, jewelry, clothing. Plus, there were two places with live music. It's not nearly as big as the Little Italy Farmer's Market, but it is nice.<//text>

<rate>5< /rate>< review>
I love this farmers market! A few blocks of a street in North Park are closed off for it, so just look for street parking in the neighborhoods (if you end up parking far, there are so many electric scooters that you can use to speed up your trek to the market. Lots of fresh produce, and fun food options. I tried the Lebanese street food stand and got a half Zaatar and half Akkawi wrap (definitely add the veggies for a $1). It was so delicious and I definitely want to try everything else on the menu.

There are a variety of food and drink options and it is also right by a lot of North Park's main businesses if you wanted to hang out there before or after your farmers market trip!<//review>

<text>We met Grayston when we walked in to check out the gym and his enthusiasm was delightful. It's a spectacular space with a welcoming feel in the common hallway and the cleanest and most spacious bathrooms, worthy of a fancy restaurant. All I do is boulder so it was really fun to try the gym out - I loved it. The pads are great, really comfy to land on. Some of the walls are pretty high so it's good to get your footing. The setting is solid, really great problems with lots of core, maneuvering, technicality, and power. My partner tried some great beginner grades and she found the V0-V2 to be pretty good. I loved the V5-7s and loved the slab wall and the overhangs. The weight room upstairs has an indoor and outdoor portion and you have the moonboard and the hangboards. The staff is great and everyone seems to be on their game when it comes to making sure to keep things clean, distanced, and masked. Parking wasn't bad for us, usually 2 hour spots available. And I think LBR has agreements with a few businesses near them to use their lots at certain hours - it's worth asking them about it. They sell chalk and chalk bags and a few other items. Can't wait for my next session.<//text>< pics>

<Name>Nathan Saltz< /Name>< review>
The setting is really good and has a nice mix of technical and pumpy, fair ratings. Really great amenities and a very unique building, the amount of climbable wall space is great. They reset once a week to keep things fresh and do not clutter the walls. The best aspect about this gym are the holds, they are the newer holds the market has, some stuff you would see on the IFSC and the friction is awesome, even their walls have grit and you can smear really well. My shoes might degrade faster though. Tall walls, so throwing to a upper hold when you feel not secure in your position feels slightly panicky, but it makes you commit to the move. Glad  they just opened, Hangar 18 has the oldest holds I've ever seen, like holding onto glass they are so polished down and greased up. Long Beach Rising is expensive, but they appear to have put a lot of money into the gym and it shows.< /review>

She and the staff were great, always smiling and warm and tolerant of our sense of humor.

Fast forward 6 months and am grateful to say my husband is healed.  Choosing Dr. Lin and working with Lisa Livian were the BEST decisions we could have made throughout my husband's road to recovery.

Lisa, you were so essential to B's healing and we are thankful beyond words for everything you did for us.  We may have started as patients but left as friends.

Love the food, but the service can be "hit or miss."  If there is a problem with the service, it's usually that our server doesn't come around.  The food is typically prepared correctly, but the server may not come around to refill drinks or fix any issue with the food until the food is cold or gone.

< Text>
Red Robin is a titan that has fallen far from where it stood. I remember 10 plus years ago when going to Red Robin filled my young heart with excitement, however, not it seems like an empty husk of its former self. The food is mediocre at best, with their menu seemingly being downsized from what it used to be. The staff seem inconvenienced to take your order, let alone bring your drinks in a timely manner. After being asked about our appetizer that we order 15 minutes prior, we were told that it would come out with our entrees, which I dont need to explain the fault of this thinking process. After our meal showed up, the last time we saw our server is when she brought the check. This is a classic case of "Dont meet your childhood heroes". Unfortunately I would recommend to avoid this chain with a 10 foot pole, far from what it used to be.< /Text>
